Prompt: 'What is considered a high blood pressure reading?\n' 
Generated text: "It should be under 160/100.  I'm surprised you've never been tested.  It's normal for a doctor to do this when you're young and healthy.  But if you have a family history or are above a certain age, it is suggested you get it tested more often."

Prompt: 'What are the risks of having high blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: '\nThe risk of heart disease is 2 to 6 times greater if you have high blood pressure, compared to people with normal blood pressure.\n\nHigh blood pressure is usually caused by an imbalance in the amount of salt in the blood (sodium). When the kidneys excrete salt, some of it stays in the body to act as a buffer against the loss of sodium and fluids (water) from the body. If this buffer is depleted, it can cause high blood pressure.\n\nWhat causes high blood pressure?\n\nHigh blood pressure is the result of a build up of pressure in the arteries and veins. This is caused by a number of factors. These include:\n\nFamily history\n\nAged 65 years and over\n\nObesity\n\nFasting glucose\n\nSmoking\n\nAlcohol consumption\n\nCardiovascular disease is a major cause of mortality, especially in older people. The following are some risk factors for cardiovascular disease:\n\nFamily history\n\nAged 65 years and over\n\nObesity\n\nDiabetes mellitus\n\nAged 45 years and over\n\nSmoking\n\nAlcohol consumption\n\nHigh blood pressure is usually inherited. However, some people develop high blood pressure from other risk factors, such as smoking.\n\nWhat are the symptoms of high blood pressure?\n\nSymptoms of high blood pressure can include:\n\nFrequent urination\n\nDizziness\n\nDry mouth\n\nNausea\n\nFatigue\n\nChest pain\n\nSudden dizziness or fainting\n\nSweating\n\nBreathlessness\n\nHeadaches\n\nDifficulty concentrating\n\nTiredness\n\nHow is high blood pressure diagnosed?\n\nHigh blood pressure is often diagnosed with a blood pressure reading.\n\nA blood pressure reading is done by taking the blood pressure of one or both arms (usually the left arm) while lying flat on your back. You may need to stand up, sit down, or use a stethoscope.\n\nThe following are the various methods that can be used to assess the blood pressure reading:\n\nAmmeter  A device that measures the force of the blood flowing through the artery. The force of the blood depends on the elasticity of the artery wall, the elasticity of the blood itself, and the pressure on the artery. A small gauge (smaller than 5mm) is used to measure the blood pressure.'

Prompt: 'What lifestyle changes can help prevent and lower high blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: "Here are some lifestyle changes you can make to help prevent high blood pressure:\n1. Eat less salt.\nThe Institute of Medicine recommends a maximum of 2,300 milligrams of sodium a day, or less than two teaspoons.\n2. Cut back on processed foods.\nThat includes hot dogs, soups, breakfast cereals, chips, crackers, and ready-to-eat foods.\n3. Get moving.\nTry to get 150 minutes of moderate-intensity activity a week, or 75 minutes of vigorous activity.\n4. Do less stress.\nThat includes managing your workload and setting limits on how many hours you spend in front of the TV.\n5. Cut back on alcohol.\nHave no more than one drink a day for women and two for men.\n6. Quit smoking.\nIt's a proven fact that smoking increases the risk of high blood pressure."

Prompt: 'What kind of medicines can help control high blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: '\nA:\n\nQuick Answer\n\nSome common medicines to help control high blood pressure include diuretics, beta-blockers and calcium channel blockers, according to WebMD. Some of these drugs are combined with a diuretic in a pill called a diuretic-beta blocker combination pill, while others are combined with a calcium channel blocker in a pill called a calcium channel blocker-beta blocker combination pill.\n\nKeep Learning\n\nDiuretics reduce the amount of water in the body, causing it to lose sodium and become more concentrated, notes the Mayo Clinic. Beta-blockers reduce the heart rate, which allows the heart to work more efficiently and reduces the amount of oxygen the heart has to use. Calcium channel blockers help relax the blood vessels, allowing more blood to move through them, according to WebMD.'

Prompt: 'What are some things that can increase the risk of getting high blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: '\nA:\n\nQuick Answer\n\nThe risk of getting high blood pressure can be increased through the consumption of junk food, smoking, not doing any physical activity, and being overweight, according to Mayo Clinic. These factors can also increase the risk of developing heart disease.\n\nKeep Learning\n\nConsuming excess salt and fat can lead to high blood pressure, according to Mayo Clinic. A high-fat diet can also increase the risk of developing diabetes, which increases the risk of high blood pressure, according to Mayo Clinic. Smoking is another risk factor that can increase the risk of high blood pressure, according to the American Heart Association.\n\nBeing overweight can also increase the risk of developing high blood pressure, according to Mayo Clinic. In addition, not doing any physical activity can increase the risk of developing high blood pressure, according to Mayo Clinic.'

If you are given a steroid to use, take it according to the directions on your prescription label.\n\nLaryngitis that is caused by bacterial or viral infections, such as the common cold, flu, or bronchitis, will not respond to treatment and will usually get better in a few days to a week.\n\nThe use of steroids may increase the risk of getting infections in the airway, and it is important to follow the instructions for taking the medication carefully.\n\nMedications such as antibiotics or antiviral medications may be given to treat bacterial infections of the larynx, and they may be given for several days or until symptoms go away.\n\nIf the laryngitis is caused by a virus, antibiotics may not be effective and may be of no benefit.\n\nHow do I treat laryngitis?\n\nStep 1\n\nTake medications to soothe the inflammation.\n\nThe medications you use depend on the specific cause of the laryngitis.\n\nTake medications that are over-the-counter (OTC) or prescribed by a doctor to treat the symptoms of the laryngitis.\n\nStep 2\n\nAvoid coughing that irritates the inflamed airway.\n\nTreatment for laryngitis usually consists of medicines that soothe the inflammation of the larynx.\n\nIf you have laryngitis, avoid coughing that irritates the inflamed airway.\n\nSome people can use a vaporizer or humidifier to help moisten the air in the room.\n\nStep 3\n\nUse moist heat packs to warm the throat.\n\nSome people find it helpful to use moist heat packs to warm the throat.\n\nThe moist heat packs may be placed on the neck or on the back of the hands.\n\nWarm the pack for a few minutes before placing it on your neck or hands.\n\nHold the pack for a few minutes and then remove it and continue to warm the neck or back of the hands for a few minutes'
